class="wt-body-max-width wt-pr-xs-2 wt-pr-lg-6 wt-pl-xs-2 wt-pl-lg-6 wt-grid"><div data-clg-id="WtGridItem" class="wt-grid__item-xs-12"><div data-clg-id="WtGrid" id="about" class="wt-bg-white wt-b-xs le-rounded-02 wt-p-xs-3 wt-p-md-5 wt-mt-xs-2 wt-grid"><div data-clg-id="WtGridItem" class="wt-grid__item-xs-12 wt-grid__item-tv-12"><div><h2 class="wt-text-title-large">About</h2><p class="wt-text-caption wt-sem-text-secondary">Tell the world all about your item and why theyll love it.</p></div><div data-clg-id="WtGridItem" class="wt-grid__item-xs-12 wt-grid__item-lg-8"><div id="field-title" class="wt-mt-md-7 wt-mt-xs-5"><label for="listing-title-input" class="wt-label wt-mb-xs-0">Title <span data-testid="required-badge" aria-hidden="true" data-required-text="Required" class="wt-label__required"></span><div data-clg-id="WtPopoverControlled" class="wt-popover"><button type="button" aria-describedby="popover-content-9b91df08-f036-4c3e-9948-471a582bd288" aria-label="Help" class="wt-popover__trigger wt-text-body-01"><span class="wt-mr-xs-1 wt-nudge-b-1 wt-icon--base-xs etsy-icon"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false"><path d="M12,22A10,10,0,1,1,22,12,10.012,10.012,0,0,1,12,22ZM12,4a8,8,0,1,0,8,8A8.009,8.009,0,0,0,12,4Z"></path><circle cx="12" cy="16.5" r="1.5"></circle><path d="M13,14H11a3.043,3.043,0,0,1,1.7-2.379C13.5,11.055,14,10.674,14,10a2,2,0,1,0-4,0H8a4,4,0,1,1,8,0,4,4,0,0,1-2.152,3.259A2.751,2.751,0,0,0,13,14Z"></path></svg></span></button><div role="tooltip" id="popover-content-9b91df08-f036-4c3e-9948-471a582bd288"><h3 class="wt-text-caption-title wt-mb-xs-1">Tips for a great title:</h3><ul class="wt-mb-xs-2"><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Clearly state the item for sale, like "mug" or "dress"</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Include the most important traits upfront, like your item's color, material, and size</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Streamline for clarity and scannability. Consider using less than 15 words when including the traits that make your item special.</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Only include holidays, special occasions, or recipient types if they're essential to what the item is, like "birthday candle" or "Halloween costume"</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Move subjective words, like "perfect" or "beautiful," to the description</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Try not to repeat words</li><li class="wt-text-caption">Don't worry about adding info about price, shipping, or sales. Etsy helps take care of this by badging your items in Search.</li></ul><p class="wt-mb-xs-2 wt-mt-xs-2 wt-text-caption">Note that the first title you publish will be used in the listing URL, even if you make edits in the future.</p><p class="wt-mb-xs-2 wt-mt-xs-2 wt-text-caption"><a data-clg-id="WtTextLink" target="_blank" href="https://www.etsy.com/seller-handbook/article/1399426136697" class="wt-sem-text-primary wt-text-link">Learn more about suggested titles<span class="wt-screen-reader-only">Opens a new tab</span></a></p><span class="wt-popover__arrow"></span></div></div></label><p id="listing-title-helper-text" class="wt-text-caption wt-display-block  wt-mb-xs-1">A good title focuses on your item and doesn't use repetitive class="wt-flex-md-1 wt-pr-md-3"><p class="wt-text-title">GPSR manufacturer and safety information</p>If youre a <a data-clg-id="WtTextLink" target="_blank" href="https://www.etsy.com/seller-handbook/article/1364599291081#TRDR" class="wt-text-link">trader<span class="wt-screen-reader-only">Opens a new tab</span></a> selling to <a data-clg-id="WtTextLink" target="_blank" href="https://www.etsy.com/seller-handbook/article/1093438529659#GPSR" class="wt-text-link">EEA states<span class="wt-screen-reader-only">Opens a new tab</span></a> or Northern Ireland (NI), you may need to include manufacturer and safety info (for listings added after December 13th, 2024) to comply with the <a data-clg-id="WtTextLink" target="_blank" href="https://www.etsy.com/seller-handbook/article/1093438529659" class="wt-text-link">General Product Safety Regulation<span class="wt-screen-reader-only">Opens a new tab</span></a> (GPSR).<br><br>You can also choose to stop selling to these states in <a data-clg-id="WtTextLink" target="_blank" href="/your/shops/me/options?ref=seller-platform-mcnav#gpsr-policy-setting-heading" class="wt-text-link">GPSR settings<span class="wt-screen-reader-only">Opens a new tab</span></a>.</div><button type="button" aria-expanded="false" data-clg-id="WtButton" class="wt-btn wt-mt-xs-4"><label for="gspr-manufacturer-info-textarea" class="wt-label wt-mb-xs-0">Manufacturers<div data-clg-id="WtPopoverControlled" class="wt-popover"><button type="button" aria-describedby="popover-content-3fefa80c-7bca-4d5e-9f22-ca7df44a5f59" aria-label="Help" class="wt-popover__trigger wt-text-body-01"><span class="wt-mr-xs-1 wt-nudge-b-1 wt-icon--base-xs id="popover-content-3fefa80c-7bca-4d5e-9f22-ca7df44a5f59"><p class="wt-mb-xs-2 wt-text-caption">The GPSR considers a manufacturer to be anyone who designs or makes a product and sells it under their name or brand.</p><p class="wt-mt-xs-2 wt-text-caption"> Selling items you designed, made, or modified? Youre probably the manufacturer.</p><p class="wt-mt-xs-2 wt-text-caption"> Selling second-hand items in their original condition? The manufacturer is likely someone else. </p><span class="wt-popover__arrow"></span></div></div></label><p id="gspr-manufacturer-info-helper-text" class="wt-text-caption wt-display-block wt-mb-xs-1">Youll need to include a name, email, and mailing address for each manufacturer. If youre a non-EU resident and make the item yourself, or you work with a non-EU manufacturer, youll need to provide the name and email of the designated EU <a data-clg-id="WtTextLink" target="_blank" href="https://www.etsy.com/seller-handbook/article/1364599291081#RES" class="wt-text-link">responsible person<span class="wt-screen-reader-only">Opens a new tab</span></a>.</p><textarea name="gpsrManufacturerContact" id="gspr-manufacturer-info-textarea" aria-invalid="false" aria-required="false" aria-describedby="gspr-manufacturer-info-helper-text" rows="6" class="wt-textarea wt-textarea" style="height: 99px !important;"></textarea></div><div id="field-gpsrSafetyWarnings" class="wt-mt-md-6 wt-mt-xs-4"><label for="gspr-safety-warnings-textarea" class="wt-label wt-mb-xs-0">Product safety info</label><p id="gspr-safety-warnings-helper-text" class="wt-text-caption wt-display-block wt-mb-xs-1">Make sure you include any safety details buyers should know like age restrictions, potential hazards, disposal instructions, etc.</p><textarea name="gpsrSafetyWarnings" id="gspr-safety-warnings-textarea" aria-invalid="false" aria-required="false" aria-describedby="gspr-safety-warnings-helper-text" rows="6" class="wt-textarea wt-textarea" style="height: 99px !important;"></textarea></div></div></div></div></div><div data-clg-id="WtGridItem" class="wt-grid__item-xs-12"><div data-clg-id="WtGrid" id="shipping" class="wt-bg-white wt-b-xs le-rounded-02 wt-p-xs-3 wt-p-md-5 wt-mt-xs-2 wt-grid"><div data-clg-id="WtGridItem" class="wt-grid__item-xs-12 wt-grid__item-tv-8"><div><h2 class="wt-text-title-large">Processing &amp;
